```python
def epigenetic_clock_analysis(methylation_data, coherence_metrics):
    """
    Correlate Horvath clock methylation markers with coherence
    """
    import numpy as np
    from scipy.stats import pearsonr
    
    # Horvath clock uses specific CpG sites
    # This is simplified
    
    # Calculate epigenetic age using Horvath algorithm
    # Placeholder
    epigenetic_age = np.mean(methylation_data, axis=1)
    
    # Correlate with coherence
    r, p = pearsonr(epigenetic_age, coherence_metrics)
    
    return {'r': r, 'p': p}


# Function 47: Sleep Spindle Density
def sleep_spindle_density(eeg_sleep, fs=256, time_hours=8):
    """
    Measure sigma-band (12-15Hz) density during NREM
    """
    from scipy.signal import butter, filtfilt
    import numpy as np
    
    # Detect NREM (simplified - would use sleep staging)
    # Placeholder - assume all data is NREM
    
    # Bandpass for sigma
    nyquist = fs / 2
    low, high = 12/nyquist, 15/nyquist
    b, a = butter(4, [low, high], btype='band')
    filtered = filtfilt(b, a, eeg_sleep)
    
    # Hilbert envelope
    from scipy.signal import hilbert
    envelope = np.abs(hilbert(filtered))
    
    # Threshold detection
    threshold = np.mean(envelope) + 2 * np.std(envelope)
    spindles = envelope > threshold
    
    # Count spindles
    transitions = np.diff(np.concatenate([[0], spindles.astype(int), [0]]))
    spindle_count = np.sum(transitions == 1)
    
    # Density per hour
    total_hours = len(eeg_sleep) / fs / 3600
    density = spindle_count / total_hours
    
    return density


# Function 48: Galvanic Skin Response Analysis
def gsr_event_analysis(gsr_signal, event_times, pre_event=2, post_event=5, fs=100):
    """
    Quantify arousal spikes before "intuitive" events
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    pre_samples = int(pre_event * fs)
    post_samples = int(post_event * fs)
    
    responses = []
    baselines = []
    
    for t in event_times:
        t_idx = int(t * fs)
        if t_idx - pre_samples < 0 or t_idx + post_samples > len(gsr_signal):
            continue
        
        baseline = np.mean(gsr_signal[t_idx-pre_samples:t_idx])
        response = np.mean(gsr_signal[t_idx:t_idx+post_samples])
        
        baselines.append(baseline)
        responses.append(response)
    
    # Test if responses > baselines
    from scipy.stats import ttest_rel
    t_stat, p_value = ttest_rel(responses, baselines)
    
    return {'t': t_stat, 'p': p_value, 
            'mean_baseline': np.mean(baselines),
            'mean_response': np.mean(responses)}


# Function 49: Drift Diffusion Model
def fit_drift_diffusion(reaction_times, accuracy, n_samples=1000):
    """
    Separate boundary separation from evidence accumulation
    """
    import numpy as np
    from scipy.optimize import minimize
    
    def neg_log_likelihood(params, rt, acc):
        v, a, t0 = params  # drift rate, boundary, non-decision time
        
        # Simplified DDM likelihood
        # Full implementation would use closed-form or simulation
        likelihood = 0
        for i in range(len(rt)):
            if acc[i] == 1:
                # Correct responses
                pred_rt = a / v + t0
            else:
                # Error responses
                pred_rt = a / (-v) + t0
            
            # Gaussian likelihood (simplified)
            likelihood += -0.5 * ((rt[i] - pred_rt) / 0.1)**2
        
        return -likelihood
    
    # Initial guess
    v0 = np.mean(accuracy) / np.mean(reaction_times)
    a0 = 1.0
    t0 = np.min(reaction_times) * 0.5
    
    result = minimize(neg_log_likelihood, [v0, a0, t0], 
                     args=(reaction_times, accuracy),
                     bounds=[(0.01, 10), (0.1, 5), (0, 0.5)])
    
    return {'v': result.x[0], 'a': result.x[1], 't0': result.x[2]}


# Function 50: Voxel-Based Morphometry
def vbm_correlation(gray_matter_density, polytope_width):
    """
    Correlate cortical thickness with Polytope width
    """
    from scipy.stats import pearsonr
    import numpy as np
    
    # Flatten gray matter images
    n_subjects = gray_matter_density.shape[0]
    n_voxels = np.prod(gray_matter_density.shape[1:])
    gm_flat = gray_matter_density.reshape(n_subjects, n_voxels)
    
    # Correlate each voxel with polytope width
    correlations = np.zeros(n_voxels)
    p_values = np.zeros(n_voxels)
    
    for v in range(n_voxels):
        r, p = pearsonr(gm_flat[:, v], polytope_width)
        correlations[v] = r
        p_values[v] = p
    
    # Reshape back to image
    corr_map = correlations.reshape(gray_matter_density.shape[1:])
    
    return corr_map, p_values


# Function 51: Cytokine Assay Analysis
def cytokine_noise_analysis(il6_levels, tnfa_levels, neural_noise):
    """
    Test inflammatory noise hypothesis
    """
    from scipy.stats import pearsonr, linregress
    import numpy as np
    
    # Multiple regression
    X = np.column_stack([il6_levels, tnfa_levels])
    from sklearn.linear_model import LinearRegression
    model = LinearRegression()
    model.fit(X, neural_noise)
    
    # Individual correlations
    r_il6, p_il6 = pearsonr(il6_levels, neural_noise)
    r_tnfa, p_tnfa = pearsonr(tnfa_levels, neural_noise)
    
    return {'r_il6': r_il6, 'p_il6': p_il6,
            'r_tnfa': r_tnfa, 'p_tnfa': p_tnfa,
            'model_r2': model.score(X, neural_noise),
            'coef_il6': model.coef_[0],
            'coef_tnfa': model.coef_[1]}


# Function 52: Rubber Hand Illusion in VR
def rubber_hand_illusion_vr(proprioceptive_drift, ownership_ratings, B_baseline):
    """
    Quantify B axis plasticity via RHI
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # RHI effect size
    drift_effect = np.mean(proprioceptive_drift)
    ownership_effect = np.mean(ownership_ratings)
    
    # Correlate with B plasticity
    B_change = B_baseline - np.mean(ownership_ratings)  # simplified
    
    return {'drift': drift_effect, 'ownership': ownership_effect,
            'B_change': B_change}


# Function 53: Stochastic Resonance Test
def stochastic_resonance_optimal(signal_detection, noise_levels):
    """
    Find optimal noise level for signal detection
    """
    import numpy as np
    from scipy.optimize import minimize_scalar
    from scipy.interpolate import interp1d
    
    # Fit SNR vs noise curve
    f = interp1d(noise_levels, signal_detection, kind='cubic')
    
    # Find maximum
    result = minimize_scalar(lambda x: -f(x), 
                            bounds=[min(noise_levels), max(noise_levels)])
    
    return {'optimal_noise': result.x, 'max_snr': -result.fun}


# Function 54: Machine Learning Decoding
def ml_decode_gnosis(eeg_features, gnosis_labels, test_size=0.2):
    """
    Train classifier to predict self-reported gnosis states
    """
    from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestClassifier
    from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split
    from sklearn.metrics import accuracy_score, roc_auc_score
    
    X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(
        eeg_features, gnosis_labels, test_size=test_size, random_state=42)
    
    # Train classifier
    clf = RandomForestClassifier(n_estimators=100, random_state=42)
    clf.fit(X_train, y_train)
    
    # Predict
    y_pred = clf.predict(X_test)
    y_prob = clf.predict_proba(X_test)
    
    accuracy = accuracy_score(y_test, y_pred)
    if len(np.unique(gnosis_labels)) == 2:
        auc = roc_auc_score(y_test, y_prob[:, 1])
    else:
        auc = None
    
    return {'accuracy': accuracy, 'auc': auc,
            'feature_importance': clf.feature_importances_}
```

### Group 4 — Rigorous Algorithms (Functions 55-72)

```python
# Function 55: Lagrangian Mind Solver
def solve_lagrangian_mind(P, B, T, potential_func, dt=0.01, n_steps=1000):
    """
    L = ½(∂P)² + ½(∂B)² + ½(∂T)² - V(P,B,T)
    Minimizes action of cognitive trajectory
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Initialize
    state = np.array([P, B, T])
    velocity = np.zeros(3)
    
    trajectory = [state.copy()]
    
    for _ in range(n_steps):
        # Compute gradient of potential
        dV = np.gradient(potential_func(state))
        
        # Euler-Lagrange update (simplified)
        acceleration = -dV
        velocity += acceleration * dt
        state += velocity * dt
        
        trajectory.append(state.copy())
    
    return np.array(trajectory)


# Function 56: Kalman Filter for P Tracking
def filter_noise_kalman(observations, process_noise=0.1, measurement_noise=1.0):
    """
    Track true state of P despite sensor noise
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    n = len(observations)
    filtered = np.zeros(n)
    P = np.zeros(n)  # estimate covariance
    
    # Initial state
    filtered[0] = observations[0]
    P[0] = measurement_noise
    
    for t in range(1, n):
        # Predict
        x_pred = filtered[t-1]
        P_pred = P[t-1] + process_noise
        
        # Update
        K = P_pred / (P_pred + measurement_noise)  # Kalman gain
        filtered[t] = x_pred + K * (observations[t] - x_pred)
        P[t] = (1 - K) * P_pred
    
    return filtered, P


# Function 57: Granger Causality Test
def compute_granger_causality_full(X, Y, max_lag=10):
    """
    Test if X Granger-causes Y
    """
    from statsmodels.tsa.stattools import grangercausalitytests
    
    data = np.column_stack([Y, X])  # Note: Y first for statsmodels
    results = grangercausalitytests(data, max_lag, verbose=False)
    
    # Extract best lag by AIC
    best_lag = None
    best_p = 1.0
    best_f = 0.0
    
    for lag in range(1, max_lag + 1):
        test_results = results[lag][0]
        f_stat = test_results['ssr_ftest'][0]
        p_val = test_results['ssr_ftest'][1]
        
        if p_val < best_p:
            best_p = p_val
            best_f = f_stat
            best_lag = lag
    
    return {'lag': best_lag, 'F': best_f, 'p': best_p}


# Function 58: Kuramoto Model Simulation
def apply_kuramoto_model(n_oscillators=100, coupling=0.5, dt=0.01, T=100):
    """
    Simulate N oscillators to find critical coupling constant K_c
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Random natural frequencies
    omega = np.random.randn(n_oscillators)
    
    # Initial phases
    theta = np.random.rand(n_oscillators) * 2 * np.pi
    
    t = np.arange(0, T, dt)
    n_steps = len(t)
    phases = np.zeros((n_steps, n_oscillators))
    phases[0] = theta
    
    order_param = np.zeros(n_steps)
    
    for i in range(1, n_steps):
        # Compute order parameter
        r = np.abs(np.mean(np.exp(1j * phases[i-1])))
        order_param[i-1] = r
        
        # Update phases
        for j in range(n_oscillators):
            sin_sum = np.sum(np.sin(phases[i-1] - phases[i-1, j]))
            phases[i, j] = phases[i-1, j] + dt * (omega[j] + coupling * sin_sum / n_oscillators)
    
    # Final order parameter
    order_param[-1] = np.abs(np.mean(np.exp(1j * phases[-1])))
    
    return phases, order_param, t


# Function 59: Effective Connectivity via DCM
def calculate_effective_connectivity_dcm_full(bold_data, design_matrix):
    """
    Full DCM would use variational Bayesian inversion
    This is a simplified spectral DCM approximation
    """
    import numpy as np
    from scipy import signal
    
    n_regions = bold_data.shape[1]
    
    # Compute cross-spectral density
    f, csd = signal.csd(bold_data.T, bold_data.T, nperseg=64)
    
    # Simplified effective connectivity via partial directed coherence
    # This is a placeholder for actual DCM
    effective_connectivity = np.zeros((n_regions, n_regions))
    
    for i in range(n_regions):
        for j in range(n_regions):
            if i != j:
                # PDC at peak frequency
                pdc = np.abs(csd[i, j]) / np.sqrt(np.abs(csd[i, i] * csd[j, j]))
                effective_connectivity[i, j] = np.max(pdc)
    
    return effective_connectivity


# Function 60: Persistent Homology for Thought Topology
def find_betti_numbers_thought(distance_matrix, max_dim=2, persistence_threshold=0.1):
    """
    Computes Betti numbers for "topology of thought"
    """
    try:
        from ripser import ripser
        import numpy as np
        
        diagrams = ripser(distance_matrix, maxdim=max_dim)['dgms']
        
        betti = []
        for dim in range(max_dim + 1):
            if dim < len(diagrams):
                persistence = diagrams[dim][:, 1] - diagrams[dim][:, 0]
                betti.append(np.sum(persistence > persistence_threshold))
            else:
                betti.append(0)
        
        return betti, diagrams
    
    except ImportError:
        print("Ripser not available. Returning placeholder.")
        return [1, 0, 0], None


# Function 61: Avalanche Size Distribution (detailed)
def detect_avalanche_size_detailed(spike_times, bin_size=0.001):
    """
    Detailed avalanche analysis with branching parameter
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Bin spikes
    max_time = np.max(spike_times)
    bins = np.arange(0, max_time + bin_size, bin_size)
    spike_counts, _ = np.histogram(spike_times, bins)
    
    # Find avalanches (consecutive non-zero bins)
    active = spike_counts > 0
    transitions = np.diff(np.concatenate([[0], active.astype(int), [0]]))
    starts = np.where(transitions == 1)[0]
    ends = np.where(transitions == -1)[0]
    
    # Avalanche properties
    sizes = []
    durations = []
    branching = []
    
    for s, e in zip(starts, ends):
        avalanche = spike_counts[s:e]
        sizes.append(np.sum(avalanche))
        durations.append(len(avalanche))
        
        # Branching parameter (ratio of spikes in next bin)
        if len(avalanche) > 1:
            branch = np.mean(avalanche[1:] / (avalanche[:-1] + 1e-10))
            branching.append(branch)
    
    # Power-law fit
    from scipy.stats import powerlaw
    
    if len(sizes) > 100:
        params = powerlaw.fit(np.array(sizes))
        ks_stat, p_val = powerlaw.fit(np.array(sizes), method='KS')
    else:
        params = [None, None]
        ks_stat = p_val = None
    
    return {'sizes': np.array(sizes),
            'durations': np.array(durations),
            'branching': np.array(branching),
            'tau': params[0] if params[0] else None,
            'ks_stat': ks_stat,
            'p_val': p_val}


# Function 62: PID Optimization for Criticality
def optimize_pid_criticality(rho_history, rho_target=1.0, dt=0.001):
    """
    Find optimal PID parameters to maintain criticality
    """
    from scipy.optimize import differential_evolution
    import numpy as np
    
    def pid_simulate(params, rho_history, dt):
        Kp, Ki, Kd = params
        error = rho_target - rho_history
        
        # Discrete PID
        integral = np.cumsum(error) * dt
        derivative = np.diff(np.concatenate([[0], error])) / dt
        
        control = Kp * error + Ki * integral + Kd * derivative
        
        # Simulated response
        rho_sim = rho_history + control
        return rho_sim
    
    def cost(params):
        rho_sim = pid_simulate(params, rho_history, dt)
        return np.mean((rho_sim - rho_target)**2)
    
    bounds = [(0, 2), (0, 1), (0, 0.5)]
    result = differential_evolution(cost, bounds, maxiter=100)
    
    return result.x, result.fun


# Function 63: Fourier Memory Retrieval
def perform_fourier_inversion_memory_full(encoding, cue):
    """
    Test if retrieval matches 2D-FFT pattern of encoding state
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Ensure 2D
    if len(encoding.shape) == 1:
        encoding = encoding.reshape(-1, 1)
    if len(cue.shape) == 1:
        cue = cue.reshape(-1, 1)
    
    # Pad to same size
    max_size = max(encoding.shape[0], cue.shape[0])
    encoding_pad = np.zeros((max_size, max_size))
    cue_pad = np.zeros((max_size, max_size))
    
    encoding_pad[:encoding.shape[0], :encoding.shape[1]] = encoding
    cue_pad[:cue.shape[0], :cue.shape[1]] = cue
    
    # 2D FFT
    F_encoding = np.fft.fft2(encoding_pad)
    F_cue = np.fft.fft2(cue_pad)
    
    # Correlation in Fourier domain
    F_retrieved = F_cue * np.conj(F_encoding)
    retrieved = np.fft.ifft2(F_retrieved)
    
    # Normalize
    retrieved = np.real(retrieved)
    retrieved = (retrieved - np.min(retrieved)) / (np.max(retrieved) - np.min(retrieved))
    
    # Compare to encoding
    encoding_norm = (encoding_pad - np.min(encoding_pad)) / (np.max(encoding_pad) - np.min(encoding_pad))
    
    similarity = np.corrcoef(retrieved.flatten(), encoding_norm.flatten())[0, 1]
    
    return retrieved, similarity


# Function 64: Mutual Information KSG (full)
def estimate_mutual_information_ksg_full(X, Y, k=3, n_shuffles=200):
    """
    Full KSG estimator for high-dimensional data
    """
    from sklearn.neighbors import NearestNeighbors
    import numpy as np
    
    X = np.array(X).reshape(-1, 1) if len(X.shape) == 1 else X
    Y = np.array(Y).reshape(-1, 1) if len(Y.shape) == 1 else Y
    
    n = len(X)
    
    # Joint space
    Z = np.column_stack([X, Y])
    
    # Nearest neighbors in joint space
    nbrs = NearestNeighbors(n_neighbors=k+1).fit(Z)
    distances, indices = nbrs.kneighbors(Z)
    epsilon = distances[:, -1]
    
    # Count neighbors in marginal spaces
    nbrs_X = NearestNeighbors(radius=np.max(distances)).fit(X)
    nbrs_Y = NearestNeighbors(radius=np.max(distances)).fit(Y)
    
    mi = 0
    for i in range(n):
        # Count neighbors in X within epsilon
        n_x = len(nbrs_X.radius_neighbors([X[i]], radius=epsilon[i])[0][0]) - 1
        n_y = len(nbrs_Y.radius_neighbors([Y[i]], radius=epsilon[i])[0][0]) - 1
        
        mi += np.log((k) / (n_x + 1)) + np.log((k) / (n_y + 1))
    
    mi = mi / n - np.log(k) * 2 + np.log(n - 1) * 2
    
    # Shuffle test
    mi_shuffled = []
    for _ in range(n_shuffles):
        Y_shuff = np.random.permutation(Y)
        mi_shuffled.append(estimate_mutual_information_ksg_full(X, Y_shuff, k, 1)[0])
    
    mi_corrected = mi - np.mean(mi_shuffled)
    p_value = np.mean(np.array(mi_shuffled) >= mi)
    
    return mi_corrected, p_value, mi_shuffled


# Function 65: Monte Carlo Permutation (full)
def run_monte_carlo_permutation_full(data, n_permutations=10000, statistic='mean'):
    """
    Create null distribution for any statistic
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    if statistic == 'mean':
        stat_fn = np.mean
    elif statistic == 'median':
        stat_fn = np.median
    elif statistic == 'std':
        stat_fn = np.std
    elif callable(statistic):
        stat_fn = statistic
    else:
        raise ValueError("statistic must be 'mean', 'median', 'std', or callable")
    
    observed = stat_fn(data)
    
    # Permutation distribution
    permuted = []
    for _ in range(n_permutations):
        shuffled = np.random.permutation(data)
        permuted.append(stat_fn(shuffled))
    
    permuted = np.array(permuted)
    
    # Two-tailed p-value
    p_value = np.mean(np.abs(permuted - np.mean(permuted)) >= 
                      np.abs(observed - np.mean(permuted)))
    
    return {'observed': observed,
            'permuted': permuted,
            'p_value': p_value,
            'ci_95': np.percentile(permuted, [2.5, 97.5])}


# Function 66: Variational Free Energy (full)
def evaluate_variational_free_energy_full(observations, predictions, complexity, temperature=1.0):
    """
    F = Complexity - Accuracy with temperature scaling
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Accuracy: negative log likelihood (Gaussian assumption)
    nll = 0.5 * np.sum((observations - predictions)**2) / temperature
    
    # Free energy
    F = complexity - nll
    
    # Model evidence
    log_evidence = -F
    
    return {'F': F, 'log_evidence': log_evidence, 'nll': nll, 'complexity': complexity}


# Function 67: Unit Balance Check (full)
def check_unit_balance_sympy_full(equation_string, unit_database=None):
    """
    Comprehensive unit consistency check
    """
    from sympy import symbols, sympify, solve, Eq
    from sympy.physics.units import mass, length, time, current, temperature
    import re
    
    # Parse equation
    left, right = equation_string.split('=')
    left_expr = sympify(left.strip())
    right_expr = sympify(right.strip())
    
    # Extract variables
    variables = set(re.findall(r'[a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]*', equation_string))
    
    # Assign units (would need database)
    # Placeholder
    units = {}
    for var in variables:
        units[var] = 'dimensionless'  # Default
    
    # Check dimensional consistency
    left_dims = 'dimensionless'  # Placeholder
    right_dims = 'dimensionless'  # Placeholder
    
    return left_dims == right_dims, {'left': left_dims, 'right': right_dims}


# Function 68: Cross-Frequency Coupling (full)
def measure_cross_frequency_coupling_full(eeg_data, fs, freq_ranges=None):
    """
    Comprehensive cross-frequency coupling analysis
    """
    from scipy.signal import butter, filtfilt, hilbert
    import numpy as np
    
    if freq_ranges is None:
        freq_ranges = {
            'delta': (0.5, 4),
            'theta': (4, 8),
            'alpha': (8, 12),
            'beta': (13, 30),
            'gamma': (30, 80)
        }
    
    nyquist = fs / 2
    results = {}
    
    # Phase-amplitude coupling for each pair
    for phase_name, (phase_low, phase_high) in freq_ranges.items():
        for amp_name, (amp_low, amp_high) in freq_ranges.items():
            if phase_name == amp_name:
                continue
            
            # Filter for phase
            b_p, a_p = butter(4, [phase_low/nyquist, phase_high/nyquist], btype='band')
            phase_signal = filtfilt(b_p, a_p, eeg_data)
            phase = np.angle(hilbert(phase_signal))
            
            # Filter for amplitude
            b_a, a_a = butter(4, [amp_low/nyquist, amp_high/nyquist], btype='band')
            amp_signal = filtfilt(b_a, a_a, eeg_data)
            amplitude = np.abs(hilbert(amp_signal))
            
            # Modulation Index
            n_bins = 18
            phase_bins = np.linspace(-np.pi, np.pi, n_bins + 1)
            phase_idx = np.digitize(phase, phase_bins) - 1
            
            mean_amp = np.zeros(n_bins)
            for i in range(n_bins):
                mean_amp[i] = np.mean(amplitude[phase_idx == i])
            
            p = mean_amp / (np.sum(mean_amp) + 1e-10)
            mi = (np.log(n_bins) + np.sum(p * np.log(p + 1e-10))) / np.log(n_bins)
            
            results[f'{phase_name}_phase_{amp_name}_amp'] = mi
    
    return results


# Function 69: Critical Slowing Down (full)
def identify_critical_slowing_down_full(time_series, window_sizes=None):
    """
    Comprehensive critical slowing down analysis
    """
    import numpy as np
    from scipy import stats
    
    if window_sizes is None:
        window_sizes = [10, 20, 30, 50, 100]
    
    results = {}
    
    for window in window_sizes:
        n_windows = len(time_series) - window
        variance = np.zeros(n_windows)
        autocorr = np.zeros(n_windows)
        skewness = np.zeros(n_windows)
        kurtosis = np.zeros(n_windows)
        
        for i in range(n_windows):
            segment = time_series[i:i+window]
            variance[i] = np.var(segment)
            autocorr[i] = np.corrcoef(segment[:-1], segment[1:])[0, 1]
            skewness[i] = stats.skew(segment)
            kurtosis[i] = stats.kurtosis(segment)
        
        # Test for trends
        x = np.arange(n_windows)
        
        results[window] = {
            'variance': {
                'slope': stats.linregress(x, variance).slope,
                'p': stats.linregress(x, variance).pvalue
            },
            'autocorr': {
                'slope': stats.linregress(x, autocorr).slope,
                'p': stats.linregress(x, autocorr).pvalue
            },
            'skewness': {
                'slope': stats.linregress(x, skewness).slope,
                'p': stats.linregress(x, skewness).pvalue
            },
            'kurtosis': {
                'slope': stats.linregress(x, kurtosis).slope,
                'p': stats.linregress(x, kurtosis).pvalue
            }
        }
    
    return results


# Function 70: Spectral Embedding for Polytope (full)
def cluster_spectral_embedding_full(eeg_data, n_components=3, n_clusters=4):
    """
    Full spectral embedding and clustering
    """
    from sklearn.manifold import SpectralEmbedding
    from sklearn.cluster import KMeans
    from sklearn.metrics import silhouette_score
    import numpy as np
    
    # Reshape: trials × features
    n_trials = eeg_data.shape[0]
    features = eeg_data.reshape(n_trials, -1)
    
    # Spectral embedding
    embedding = SpectralEmbedding(n_components=n_components, random_state=42)
    projected = embedding.fit_transform(features)
    
    # Cluster in embedded space
    kmeans = KMeans(n_clusters=n_clusters, random_state=42, n_init=10)
    labels = kmeans.fit_predict(projected)
    
    # Evaluate clustering
    silhouette = silhouette_score(projected, labels)
    
    return {'projected': projected,
            'labels': labels,
            'silhouette': silhouette,
            'cluster_centers': kmeans.cluster_centers_,
            'embedding_matrix': embedding.embedding_}


# Function 71: Renyi Entropy (full)
def calculate_renyi_entropy_full(data, alpha_range=[0.5, 1, 2, 3, 5, 10], bins='auto'):
    """
    Renyi entropy for multiple alpha values
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    hist, bin_edges = np.histogram(data, bins=bins, density=True)
    p = hist[hist > 0]
    
    results = {}
    
    for alpha in alpha_range:
        if alpha == 1:
            # Shannon entropy (limit as α→1)
            H = -np.sum(p * np.log(p))
        else:
            H = (1/(1-alpha)) * np.log(np.sum(p**alpha))
        
        results[alpha] = H
    
    return results


# Function 72: Lindblad Master Equation (full)
def solve_lindblad_master_eq_full(H, collapse_ops, gamma_vals, rho0, t_span, n_steps=1000):
    """
    Full Lindblad equation solver with multiple collapse operators
    """
    from scipy.integrate import solve_ivp
    import numpy as np
    
    n = H.shape[0]
    t_eval = np.linspace(t_span[0], t_span[1], n_steps)
    
    def lindblad_rhs(t, rho_vec):
        rho = rho_vec.reshape(n, n)
        
        # Unitary evolution
        drho = -1j * (H @ rho - rho @ H)
        
        # Dissipative terms
        for L, gamma in zip(collapse_ops, gamma_vals):
            L_dag = L.conj().T
            drho += gamma * (L @ rho @ L_dag - 0.5 * (L_dag @ L @ rho + rho @ L_dag @ L))
        
        return drho.flatten()
    
    rho0_vec = rho0.flatten()
    sol = solve_ivp(lindblad_rhs, t_span, rho0_vec, t_eval=t_eval, method='RK45')
    
    # Reshape solution
    n_times = len(sol.t)
    rho_t = sol.y.T.reshape(n_times, n, n)
    
    # Compute purity and other metrics
    purity = np.zeros(n_times)
    for i in range(n_times):
        purity[i] = np.trace(rho_t[i] @ rho_t[i]).real
    
    return {'t': sol.t, 'rho': rho_t, 'purity': purity}
```

### Group 5 — Advanced Algorithms (Functions 73-90)

```python
# Function 73: Five-Factor Personality Mapping
def map_ocean_to_pbt(ocean_scores):
    """
    Map OCEAN personality factors to P-B-T axes
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Mapping matrix from OCEAN to P-B-T
    # Based on theoretical relationships
    mapping_matrix = np.array([
        [0.8, 0.2, -0.3, 0.1, 0.4],   # P weights
        [-0.2, 0.7, 0.3, -0.5, 0.2],  # B weights
        [0.1, -0.1, 0.6, 0.2, -0.7]    # T weights
    ])
    
    # OCEAN order: Openness, Conscientiousness, Extraversion, Agreeableness, Neuroticism
    ocean = np.array(ocean_scores)
    
    pbt = mapping_matrix @ ocean
    
    return {'P': pbt[0], 'B': pbt[1], 'T': pbt[2]}


# Function 74: Neurotransmitter Precision Mapping
def neurotransmitter_precision_mapping(da_level, ht_level, ne_level, gaba_level):
    """
    P = P0 + α_DA[DA] - β_5HT[5HT] + γ_NE[NE] - δ_GABA[GABA]
    """
    # Default parameters (would be calibrated from data)
    P0 = 1.0
    alpha_DA = 0.5
    beta_5HT = 0.3
    gamma_NE = 0.4
    delta_GABA = 0.6
    
    P = (P0 + alpha_DA * da_level - beta_5HT * ht_level + 
         gamma_NE * ne_level - delta_GABA * gaba_level)
    
    return max(0.1, P)  # Ensure positive


# Function 75: Stress-Induced Boundary Collapse
def stress_boundary_collapse(B0, stress_time_series, k=0.1, B_min=0.1):
    """
    B(t) = B0·exp(-k∫S(τ)dτ) + B_min(1 - exp(-k∫S))
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    cumulative_stress = np.cumsum(stress_time_series)
    exp_factor = np.exp(-k * cumulative_stress)
    
    B_t = B0 * exp_factor + B_min * (1 - exp_factor)
    
    return B_t


# Function 76: Temporal Discounting with Precision
def temporal_discounting_precision(delay, reward, P, P0=1.0, k=0.1):
    """
    V(t) = A / (1 + kt)^(P/P0)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    exponent = P / P0
    value = reward / (1 + k * delay) ** exponent
    
    return value


# Function 77: Federated Coherence Gradient Descent
def federated_coherence_gradient_descent(W_A, W_B, F_A, F_B, F_AB, alpha=0.01, n_iter=100):
    """
    Each node updates weights to minimize own and dyadic free energy
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    W_A_opt = W_A.copy()
    W_B_opt = W_B.copy()
    
    loss_history = []
    
    for i in range(n_iter):
        # Compute gradients (simplified)
        grad_A = 2 * (W_A_opt - W_A) + alpha * 2 * (F_AB - F_A - F_B) * (W_A_opt - W_B_opt)
        grad_B = 2 * (W_B_opt - W_B) + alpha * 2 * (F_AB - F_A - F_B) * (W_B_opt - W_A_opt)
        
        # Update
        W_A_opt -= 0.01 * grad_A
        W_B_opt -= 0.01 * grad_B
        
        # Compute loss
        loss = (np.sum((W_A_opt - W_A)**2) + np.sum((W_B_opt - W_B)**2) + 
                alpha * (F_AB - F_A - F_B)**2)
        loss_history.append(loss)
    
    return W_A_opt, W_B_opt, loss_history


# Function 78: Holographic Memory Retrieval
def holographic_memory_retrieval(memory_hologram, cue):
    """
    M_retrieved = F^(-1)(F(Cue) · F(Memory_Hologram))
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Ensure same size
    if len(memory_hologram) != len(cue):
        # Pad to larger size
        n = max(len(memory_hologram), len(cue))
        memory_pad = np.zeros(n)
        cue_pad = np.zeros(n)
        memory_pad[:len(memory_hologram)] = memory_hologram
        cue_pad[:len(cue)] = cue
    else:
        memory_pad = memory_hologram
        cue_pad = cue
    
    # Fourier domain correlation
    F_memory = np.fft.fft(memory_pad)
    F_cue = np.fft.fft(cue_pad)
    F_retrieved = F_cue * np.conj(F_memory)
    retrieved = np.fft.ifft(F_retrieved)
    
    return np.real(retrieved)


# Function 79: Criticality Homeostasis PID Controller
def criticality_homeostasis_pid(rho_measured, rho_target=1.0, dt=0.001, 
                                Kp=1.0, Ki=0.1, Kd=0.05):
    """
    PID controller maintaining ρ near target
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    n = len(rho_measured)
    control = np.zeros(n)
    integral = 0
    prev_error = 0
    
    for t in range(n):
        error = rho_target - rho_measured[t]
        integral += error * dt
        derivative = (error - prev_error) / dt
        
        control[t] = Kp * error + Ki * integral + Kd * derivative
        
        prev_error = error
    
    return control


# Function 80: Bayesian Boundary Update
def bayesian_boundary_update(prior_self, likelihood, observation, B):
    """
    P(self|obs)_{t+1} = [P(obs|self)P(self)_t / P(obs)] * e^(-B)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Bayes update
    posterior = prior_self * likelihood / (prior_self * likelihood + 
                                           (1-prior_self) * (1-likelihood) + 1e-10)
    
    # Boundary modulation
    posterior_boundary = posterior * np.exp(-B)
    
    # Renormalize
    posterior_boundary = posterior_boundary / (posterior_boundary + (1 - posterior))
    
    return posterior_boundary


# Function 81: Temporal Horizon Integration
def temporal_horizon_integration(memory, predictions, w_memory=0.5, w_future=0.5, gamma=0.1):
    """
    H(t) = ∫ w(t-τ)M(τ)dτ + ∫ e^(-γ(τ-t))E[M(τ)]dτ
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    n = len(memory)
    horizon = np.zeros(n)
    
    for t in range(n):
        # Past integration (memory)
        past_integral = 0
        for tau in range(t):
            past_integral += w_memory * np.exp(-(t-tau)) * memory[tau]
        
        # Future integration (predictions)
        future_integral = 0
        for tau in range(t, n):
            future_integral += w_future * np.exp(-gamma * (tau - t)) * predictions[tau]
        
        horizon[t] = past_integral + future_integral
    
    return horizon


# Function 82: Coherence Polytope Monitor
def check_polytope_stability(sigma, rho, r, d_s, sigma_max=8.2, rho_max=0.95, r_max=0.93):
    """
    Real-time boundary checks for safe cognitive operation
    """
    alerts = []
    
    if sigma > sigma_max:
        alerts.append(f"NOISE_ALERT: σ={sigma:.2f} > {sigma_max}")
    
    if rho > rho_max:
        alerts.append(f"CHAOS_RISK: ρ={rho:.3f} > {rho_max}")
    
    if rho < 0.85:
        alerts.append(f"RIGIDITY_RISK: ρ={rho:.3f} < 0.85")
    
    if r/d_s > r_max:
        alerts.append(f"OVERLOAD_RISK: r/d_s={r/d_s:.3f} > {r_max}")
    
    if r/d_s < 0.72:
        alerts.append(f"COLLAPSE_RISK: r/d_s={r/d_s:.3f} < 0.72")
    
    stable = (sigma < sigma_max and rho < rho_max and r/d_s < r_max)
    
    return stable, alerts


# Function 83: Psychic Accuracy Predictor
def predict_psychic_accuracy(P, B, T, sigma, sigma0=5.0, Trange=2.0):
    """
    Acc = P/(1+B²) · e^(-σ/σ₀) · (1 - |T - T_actual|/T_range)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Placeholder for actual T (would need target)
    T_actual = 0
    
    term1 = P / (1 + B**2)
    term2 = np.exp(-sigma / sigma0)
    term3 = 1 - np.abs(T - T_actual) / Trange
    
    accuracy = term1 * term2 * term3
    
    # Clip to [0, 1]
    accuracy = np.clip(accuracy, 0, 1)
    
    return accuracy


# Function 84: Attractor Basin Depth
def calculate_attractor_basin_depth(free_energy_landscape, x_min):
    """
    D_basin = ∂²F/∂x² at x_min
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Find index nearest to minimum
    idx = np.argmin(np.abs(np.arange(len(free_energy_landscape)) - x_min))
    
    if idx == 0 or idx == len(free_energy_landscape) - 1:
        return np.inf  # at boundary
    
    # Second derivative via finite differences
    second_deriv = (free_energy_landscape[idx+1] - 2*free_energy_landscape[idx] + 
                    free_energy_landscape[idx-1])
    
    return second_deriv


# Function 85: Phase Transition Thermodynamic Trigger
def phase_transition_trigger(dE, dS, Omega_f, Omega_i, k_B=1.38e-23):
    """
    T_transition = ΔE/ΔS · 1/(k_B ln(Ω_f/Ω_i))
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    if Omega_f <= Omega_i:
        return np.inf  # no transition
    
    T = (dE / dS) * 1 / (k_B * np.log(Omega_f / Omega_i))
    
    return T


# Function 86: Holographic Compression Ratio
def holographic_compression_ratio(n_states):
    """
    η_holographic = 1 / log₂(N_states)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    if n_states <= 1:
        return 1.0
    
    ratio = 1.0 / np.log2(n_states)
    
    return ratio


# Function 87: Spectral Radius from Connectivity
def spectral_radius_from_connectivity(connectivity_matrix):
    """
    ρ(W) = max |λ_i|
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    eigenvalues = np.linalg.eigvals(connectivity_matrix)
    rho = np.max(np.abs(eigenvalues))
    
    return rho


# Function 88: Update Time from EEG
def estimate_update_time_eeg(eeg_data, fs):
    """
    τ_u ≈ (1/f_dominant) · (PLV / ITR)
    """
    from scipy import signal
    import numpy as np
    
    # Dominant frequency
    f, psd = signal.welch(eeg_data, fs, nperseg=fs*2)
    f_dominant = f[np.argmax(psd)]
    
    # Phase-locking value (simplified - average over channels)
    n_channels = eeg_data.shape[1]
    plv_sum = 0
    for i in range(n_channels):
        for j in range(i+1, n_channels):
            phase_i = np.angle(signal.hilbert(eeg_data[:, i]))
            phase_j = np.angle(signal.hilbert(eeg_data[:, j]))
            plv = np.abs(np.mean(np.exp(1j * (phase_i - phase_j))))
            plv_sum += plv
    
    mean_plv = plv_sum / (n_channels * (n_channels-1) / 2)
    
    # Information transfer rate (placeholder)
    itr = 1.0
    
    tau_u = (1 / f_dominant) * (mean_plv / itr)
    
    return tau_u


# Function 89: Boundary Strength from Connectivity
def boundary_strength_from_connectivity(dmn_internal, dmn_external, oxytocin_level):
    """
    B = (FC_DMN-internal / FC_DMN-external) · 1/(1 + oxytocin)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    B = (dmn_internal / (dmn_external + 1e-10)) / (1 + oxytocin_level)
    
    return B


# Function 90: Noise Tolerance Estimation
def estimate_noise_tolerance(P, P_max=3.0, snr_critical=1.0, baseline_snr=2.0):
    """
    σ_max = (SNR_critical / baseline_SNR) · (P_max / P)
    """
    sigma_max = (snr_critical / baseline_snr) * (P_max / P)
    
    return sigma_max
```

### Group 6 — Transfer and Network Functions (Functions 91-108)

```python
# Function 91: Coherence Transfer Function
def coherence_transfer(source_CI, t, tau_coupling, B):
    """
    CI_transferred = CI_source · (1 - e^(-t/τ_coupling)) · e^(-B)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    CI_trans = source_CI * (1 - np.exp(-t / tau_coupling)) * np.exp(-B)
    
    return CI_trans


# Function 92: Emotional Contagion PDE Solver
def solve_emotional_contagion(initial_emotion, D=0.1, tau_decay=10, alpha=1.0, 
                              source_positions=None, source_strengths=None,
                              dx=0.1, dt=0.01, n_steps=1000):
    """
    ∂E/∂t = D∇²E - E/τ_decay + α Σ δ(r - r_i)E_i
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    n_space = len(initial_emotion)
    E = initial_emotion.copy()
    history = [E.copy()]
    
    for step in range(n_steps):
        # Diffusion (simplified 1D)
        laplacian = np.zeros_like(E)
        laplacian[1:-1] = (E[2:] - 2*E[1:-1] + E[:-2]) / dx**2
        
        # Decay
        decay = E / tau_decay
        
        # Sources
        sources = np.zeros_like(E)
        if source_positions is not None and source_strengths is not None:
            for pos, strength in zip(source_positions, source_strengths):
                idx = int(pos / dx)
                if 0 <= idx < len(E):
                    sources[idx] += alpha * strength
        
        # Update
        E += dt * (D * laplacian - decay + sources)
        
        # Boundary conditions (zero flux)
        E[0] = E[1]
        E[-1] = E[-2]
        
        history.append(E.copy())
    
    return np.array(history)


# Function 93: Memory Consolidation Integral
def memory_consolidation_integral(short_term_memory, sleep_spindle_kernel, sleep_time):
    """
    M_long-term = ∫_sleep K(t) · M_short-term(t) dt
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Ensure same length
    min_len = min(len(short_term_memory), len(sleep_spindle_kernel))
    memory = short_term_memory[:min_len]
    kernel = sleep_spindle_kernel[:min_len]
    
    # Convolution integral
    consolidated = np.convolve(memory, kernel, mode='same') * sleep_time / min_len
    
    return consolidated


# Function 94: Predictive Coding Hierarchy
def predictive_coding_hierarchy(sensory_input, hierarchy_levels=3, n_iter=100):
    """
    Hierarchical prediction error minimization
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Initialize representations
    mu = [np.random.randn(len(sensory_input)) for _ in range(hierarchy_levels)]
    
    # Generate models (random for demo)
    def g(mu_next):
        return mu_next * 0.5  # simplified
    
    # Learning rates
    kappa = [0.1, 0.05, 0.01]
    
    history = []
    
    for _ in range(n_iter):
        # Bottom-up: compute prediction errors
        errors = []
        for level in range(hierarchy_levels):
            if level == 0:
                # Sensory level
                pred = g(mu[1])
                error = mu[0] - pred
            elif level == hierarchy_levels - 1:
                # Top level
                pred = 0  # prior
                error = mu[level] - pred
            else:
                # Hidden levels
                pred_up = g(mu[level+1])
                pred_down = g(mu[level])  # for top-down
                error = mu[level] - pred_up
        
        # Update representations
        for level in range(hierarchy_levels):
            if level == 0:
                mu[level] -= kappa[level] * errors[level]
            elif level == hierarchy_levels - 1:
                mu[level] -= kappa[level] * errors[level]
            else:
                mu[level] -= kappa[level] * (errors[level] + errors[level-1])
        
        history.append([m.copy() for m in mu])
    
    return mu, history


# Function 95: Free Energy Decomposition
def decompose_free_energy(q_z, p_z, p_x_z, observations):
    """
    F = D_KL[q(z)||p(z)] + E_q[-ln p(x|z)]
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Complexity: KL divergence
    complexity = np.sum(q_z * np.log(q_z / (p_z + 1e-10) + 1e-10))
    
    # Inaccuracy: expected negative log likelihood
    inaccuracy = -np.sum(q_z * np.log(p_x_z + 1e-10))
    
    F = complexity + inaccuracy
    
    return {'F': F, 'complexity': complexity, 'inaccuracy': inaccuracy}


# Function 96: Social Inference Bayesian Network
def social_inference_bayesian_network(observations, prior_A, prior_B, likelihood):
    """
    P(M_A, M_B|O) ∝ P(O|M_A,M_B)P(M_A)P(M_B)P(M_A,M_B)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    n_states_A = len(prior_A)
    n_states_B = len(prior_B)
    
    posterior = np.zeros((n_states_A, n_states_B))
    
    for a in range(n_states_A):
        for b in range(n_states_B):
            posterior[a, b] = (likelihood[a, b] * prior_A[a] * prior_B[b] * 
                              np.exp(-np.abs(a-b)/10))  # simplified coupling
    
    # Normalize
    posterior = posterior / np.sum(posterior)
    
    # Marginals
    marginal_A = np.sum(posterior, axis=1)
    marginal_B = np.sum(posterior, axis=0)
    
    return {'posterior': posterior, 'marginal_A': marginal_A, 'marginal_B': marginal_B}


# Function 97: Attentional Field Equation
def attentional_field_equation(initial_attention, source_input, alpha=0.1, beta=0.01, gamma=1.0,
                               dx=0.1, dt=0.01, n_steps=100):
    """
    ∂A/∂t = α∇²A - βA + γI(x,t)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    n_space = len(initial_attention)
    A = initial_attention.copy()
    history = [A.copy()]
    
    for step in range(n_steps):
        # Diffusion
        laplacian = np.zeros_like(A)
        laplacian[1:-1] = (A[2:] - 2*A[1:-1] + A[:-2]) / dx**2
        
        # Decay
        decay = beta * A
        
        # Source input at current time
        if step < len(source_input):
            I = source_input[step]
        else:
            I = np.zeros_like(A)
        
        # Update
        A += dt * (alpha * laplacian - decay + gamma * I)
        
        # Boundary conditions (zero flux)
        A[0] = A[1]
        A[-1] = A[-2]
        
        history.append(A.copy())
    
    return np.array(history)


# Function 98: Neuromodulatory Gain Control
def neuromodulatory_gain_control(x, da_level, ne_level, x0=0, g_da=1.0, g_ne=1.0):
    """
    f_gain(x) = 1/(1 + e^(-(g_DA[DA] + g_NE[NE])(x - x0)))
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    gain = g_da * da_level + g_ne * ne_level
    f = 1 / (1 + np.exp(-gain * (x - x0)))
    
    return f


# Function 99: Stress-Allostasis Coupling
def stress_allostasis_coupling(stress_input, recovery_input, initial_al=0, k1=0.1, k2=0.05, k3=0.01):
    """
    dAL/dt = k1·S(t) - k2·R(t) - k3·AL
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    n = len(stress_input)
    al = np.zeros(n)
    al[0] = initial_al
    
    for t in range(1, n):
        al[t] = al[t-1] + k1 * stress_input[t] - k2 * recovery_input[t] - k3 * al[t-1]
    
    return al


# Function 100: Circadian Phase Equation
def circadian_phase_equation(initial_phase, light_input, social_input, 
                            omega0=2*np.pi/24, K_light=0.1, K_social=0.05, dt=0.1):
    """
    dφ/dt = ω₀ + K_light sin(φ_light - φ) + K_social sin(φ_social - φ)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    n = len(light_input)
    phase = np.zeros(n)
    phase[0] = initial_phase
    
    for t in range(1, n):
        light_term = K_light * np.sin(light_input[t] - phase[t-1])
        social_term = K_social * np.sin(social_input[t] - phase[t-1])
        
        phase[t] = phase[t-1] + dt * (omega0 + light_term + social_term)
    
    return phase


# Function 101: Neuroplasticity Learning Rule
def neuroplasticity_learning_rule(pre_activity, post_activity, w_init, eta=0.01, beta=0.001, 
                                  bdnf_factor=1.0, tau_crit=100):
    """
    Δw_ij = η(x_i x_j - β w_ij) + γ·BDNF·e^(-t/τ_crit)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    n = len(pre_activity)
    w = w_init.copy()
    w_history = [w.copy()]
    
    for t in range(1, n):
        # Hebbian term
        hebbian = eta * (pre_activity[t] * post_activity[t] - beta * w)
        
        # BDNF modulation (critical period)
        bdnf_term = bdnf_factor * np.exp(-t / tau_crit)
        
        # Update
        w += hebbian + bdnf_term
        
        # Keep bounded
        w = np.clip(w, 0, 1)
        
        w_history.append(w.copy())
    
    return np.array(w_history)


# Function 102: Mitochondrial Energy Budget
def mitochondrial_energy_budget(oxphos_rate, demand_rate, E_min=0.1):
    """
    E_ATP = ∫(P_oxphos - P_demand) dt, subject to E_ATP > E_min
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    n = len(oxphos_rate)
    E_ATP = np.zeros(n)
    
    for t in range(1, n):
        E_ATP[t] = E_ATP[t-1] + (oxphos_rate[t] - demand_rate[t])
        
        # Enforce minimum
        if E_ATP[t] < E_min:
            E_ATP[t] = E_min
    
    return E_ATP


# Function 103: Integrated Information (Φ) Approximation
def integrated_information_approximation(connectivity_matrix, n_partitions=100):
    """
    Φ = min_partition ½ Σ I(X_k; X - X_k)
    Simplified approximation
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    n = connectivity_matrix.shape[0]
    
    # Generate random partitions
    min_phi = np.inf
    
    for _ in range(n_partitions):
        # Random bipartition
        part = np.random.choice([0, 1], n)
        if np.sum(part) == 0 or np.sum(part) == n:
            continue
        
        # Mutual information approximation using connectivity
        within_A = connectivity_matrix[np.ix_(part==0, part==0)]
        within_B = connectivity_matrix[np.ix_(part==1, part==1)]
        between = connectivity_matrix[np.ix_(part==0, part==1)]
        
        # Effective information
        phi_A = np.sum(np.abs(within_A)) - np.sum(np.abs(between)) / 2
        phi_B = np.sum(np.abs(within_B)) - np.sum(np.abs(between)) / 2
        
        phi = (phi_A + phi_B) / 2
        
        if phi < min_phi:
            min_phi = phi
    
    return max(0, min_phi)


# Function 104: Psychic Signal Detection Theory
def psychic_signal_detection_theory(mu_signal, mu_noise, sigma_signal, sigma_noise, P, P0=1.0):
    """
    d' = (μ_signal - μ_noise) / √(0.5(σ_signal² + σ_noise²)) · (P/P₀)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    d_prime = ((mu_signal - mu_noise) / np.sqrt(0.5 * (sigma_signal**2 + sigma_noise**2)) * 
               (P / P0))
    
    return d_prime


# Function 105: Markov Blanket Information Flow
def markov_blanket_information_flow(sensory_input, internal_state, external_state, action):
    """
    I_in = I(S; Internal|External)
    I_out = I(Action; External|Internal)
    """
    from sklearn.feature_selection import mutual_info_regression
    import numpy as np
    
    # Reshape for sklearn
    S = sensory_input.reshape(-1, 1)
    I = internal_state.reshape(-1, 1)
    E = external_state.reshape(-1, 1)
    A = action.reshape(-1, 1)
    
    # Conditional mutual information approximations
    # I(S; I | E)
    mi_si = mutual_info_regression(S, I.flatten())[0]
    mi_se = mutual_info_regression(S, E.flatten())[0]
    mi_si_given_e = mi_si - mi_se  # approximation
    
    # I(A; E | I)
    mi_ae = mutual_info_regression(A, E.flatten())[0]
    mi_ai = mutual_info_regression(A, I.flatten())[0]
    mi_ae_given_i = mi_ae - mi_ai  # approximation
    
    return {'I_in': mi_si_given_e, 'I_out': mi_ae_given_i}


# Function 106: Coherence Decay Spectrum
def coherence_decay_spectrum(coherence_time_series, dt=0.001, n_components=5):
    """
    CI(t) = Σ A_i e^(-t/τ_i) cos(ω_i t + φ_i)
    """
    from scipy.optimize import curve_fit
    import numpy as np
    
    def multi_exp_cos(t, *params):
        n = len(params) // 4
        result = np.zeros_like(t)
        for i in range(n):
            A = params[4*i]
            tau = params[4*i + 1]
            omega = params[4*i + 2]
            phi = params[4*i + 3]
            result += A * np.exp(-t/tau) * np.cos(omega * t + phi)
        return result
    
    t = np.arange(len(coherence_time_series)) * dt
    
    # Initial guess
    p0 = []
    for i in range(n_components):
        p0.extend([1.0, 0.1, 10.0, 0.0])
    
    try:
        popt, _ = curve_fit(multi_exp_cos, t[:len(coherence_time_series)], 
                            coherence_time_series, p0=p0, maxfev=5000)
        
        # Extract parameters
        params = []
        for i in range(n_components):
            params.append({
                'A': popt[4*i],
                'tau': popt[4*i + 1],
                'omega': popt[4*i + 2],
                'phi': popt[4*i + 3]
            })
        
        return params
    except:
        return None


# Function 107: Fractal Self-Similarity Scaling
def fractal_self_similarity_scaling(P_values, B_values, T_values, scales):
    """
    P(L) = P₀ L^(D_P - 3)
    B(L) = B₀ L^(D_B - 3)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Log-log regression for each axis
    def fit_fractal(values, scales):
        log_scales = np.log(scales)
        log_values = np.log(values)
        
        coeffs = np.polyfit(log_scales, log_values, 1)
        D = coeffs[0] + 3  # exponent + dimension
        
        return D, coeffs
    
    D_P, coeffs_P = fit_fractal(P_values, scales)
    D_B, coeffs_B = fit_fractal(B_values, scales)
    D_T, coeffs_T = fit_fractal(T_values, scales)
    
    return {'D_P': D_P, 'D_B': D_B, 'D_T': D_T,
            'coeffs_P': coeffs_P, 'coeffs_B': coeffs_B, 'coeffs_T': coeffs_T}


# Function 108: Unified Diagnostic Algorithm
def unified_diagnostic(P, B, T, sigma, rho, r, d_s):
    """
    Decision-tree classifier mapping coordinates to DSM-compatible diagnoses
    """
    diagnostics = []
    
    # Check each condition
    if P > 2.0 and B < -1.5:
        diagnostics.append("schizophrenia_spectrum")
    elif P > 1.5 and B > 1.0 and T < -2.0:
        diagnostics.append("PTSD")
    elif P > 1.5 and B > 1.0 and T > 2.0:
        diagnostics.append("OCD")
    elif P < -1.5 and abs(B) < 0.5 and abs(T) < 0.5:
        diagnostics.append("ADHD")
    elif P < -1.5 and T < -1.0:
        diagnostics.append("depression")
    elif abs(P) < 1.0 and B < -1.5 and abs(T) < 1.0:
        diagnostics.append("BPD")
    elif abs(P) < 0.5 and B > 2.0 and T > 1.0:
        diagnostics.append("psychopathy")
    
    # Check polytope violations
    if sigma > 8.2:
        diagnostics.append("elevated_noise")
    if rho > 0.95:
        diagnostics.append("chaos_risk")
    if r/d_s > 0.93:
        diagnostics.append("overload_risk")
    
    if not diagnostics:
        diagnostics.append("within_normal_range")
    
    return diagnostics
```

### Group 7 — Unified Formalizations (Functions 109-126)

```python
# Function 109: Unified Field Theory of Mind
def unified_field_theory_mind(P_field, B_field, T_field, W_field, C_field, g_metric):
    """
    ℒ_mind = ½(∂P)² + ½(∂B)² + ½(∂T)² - V(P,B,T) + ℒ_CC(λ,T_c,τ_u) + ℒ_UHIF(W,C,S)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Kinetic terms
    dP_dt = np.gradient(P_field)
    dB_dt = np.gradient(B_field)
    dT_dt = np.gradient(T_field)
    
    kinetic = 0.5 * (dP_dt**2 + dB_dt**2 + dT_dt**2)
    
    # Potential (simplified harmonic)
    V = 0.5 * (P_field**2 + B_field**2 + T_field**2)
    
    # CC term (placeholder)
    lambda_val = 1.0
    T_c = 1.0
    tau_u = 1.0
    L_CC = lambda_val * T_c / tau_u
    
    # UHIF term (placeholder)
    S = np.random.randn(*W_field.shape) * 0.1
    R = np.tanh(W_field @ C_field + S)
    L_UHIF = -np.sum(R**2)
    
    # Total Lagrangian
    L = kinetic - V + L_CC + L_UHIF
    
    return L


# Function 110: Master Equation of Consciousness
def master_equation_consciousness(rho_mind, H_corr, L_ops, gamma_vals, D_fed_strength=0.1, dt=0.01, n_steps=1000):
    """
    dρ/dt = -i[H,ρ] + Σ γ_k(L_k ρ L_k† - ½{L_k†L_k, ρ}) + D_fed(ρ)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    n = rho_mind.shape[0]
    n_steps = n_steps
    rho_history = [rho_mind.copy()]
    
    for step in range(n_steps):
        # Unitary evolution
        drho = -1j * (H_corr @ rho_mind - rho_mind @ H_corr)
        
        # Dissipative terms
        for L, gamma in zip(L_ops, gamma_vals):
            L_dag = L.conj().T
            drho += gamma * (L @ rho_mind @ L_dag - 
                            0.5 * (L_dag @ L @ rho_mind + rho_mind @ L_dag @ L))
        
        # Federated coupling (simplified - coupling to environment)
        rho_env = np.eye(n) / n  # maximally mixed environment
        D_fed = D_fed_strength * (rho_env - rho_mind)
        drho += D_fed
        
        # Update
        rho_mind = rho_mind + dt * drho
        
        # Ensure Hermitian and trace 1
        rho_mind = (rho_mind + rho_mind.conj().T) / 2
        rho_mind = rho_mind / np.trace(rho_mind)
        
        rho_history.append(rho_mind.copy())
    
    return np.array(rho_history)


# Function 111: Einstein-Information Field Equations
def einstein_information_field_equations(T_matter, T_info, T_coherence, G=1.0, Lambda=0.0):
    """
    G_μν + Λg_μν = 8πG(T_matter + T_info + T_coherence)
    Simplified 2D placeholder
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # This is a placeholder - actual GR solutions require complex numerics
    # For demonstration, compute scalar curvature analog
    
    # Energy-momentum tensors
    T_total = T_matter + T_info + T_coherence
    
    # Simplified curvature (trace of Einstein tensor ≈ -R/2 in 2D)
    R = -2 * 8 * np.pi * G * np.trace(T_total) + 2 * Lambda
    
    # Metric perturbation (simplified)
    g = np.eye(len(T_total)) * (1 + R/10)
    
    return g, R


# Function 112: Holographic Principle for Mind
def holographic_mind_bound(cortical_area, P, B, l_P=1.0, P0=1.0):
    """
    S_mind ≤ (A_cortical / 4l_P²) · (P/P₀) · e^(-B)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Holographic bound
    bound = (cortical_area / (4 * l_P**2)) * (P / P0) * np.exp(-B)
    
    return bound


# Function 113: Unified Free Energy Action
def unified_free_energy_action(F_i, F_ij, curvature_term, g_metric, R):
    """
    F_total = Σ F_i + Σ F_ij + ∫ d⁴x √(-g)(R/16πG + ℒ_corr)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Individual free energies
    sum_individual = np.sum(F_i)
    
    # Dyadic couplings
    sum_dyadic = np.sum(F_ij)
    
    # Spacetime term (simplified - integrate over grid)
    g_det = np.linalg.det(g_metric)
    spacetime_term = np.sum(np.sqrt(-g_det) * (R / (16 * np.pi) + 1.0))
    
    F_total = sum_individual + sum_dyadic + spacetime_term
    
    return F_total


# Function 114: Conservation of Coherence (Extended H13-H15)
def conservation_of_coherence(CI_B, CI_C, CI_S, CI_Q, CI_net, CI_social, 
                             sigma_topo, sigma_pol, sigma_bio):
    """
    ∂_t(Σ CI) = σ_topo + σ_pol + σ_bio
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    total_CI = (np.sum(CI_B) + np.sum(CI_C) + np.sum(CI_S) + np.sum(CI_Q) + 
                CI_net + CI_social)
    
    d_total_dt = sigma_topo + sigma_pol + sigma_bio
    
    return total_CI, d_total_dt


# Function 115: Relational Quantum Field Theory Path Integral
def relational_qft_path_integral(P_configs, B_configs, T_configs, W_configs, C_configs, action_S):
    """
    Z = ∫ 𝒟[P]𝒟[B]𝒟[T]𝒟[W]𝒟[C] e^{iS}
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # This is a placeholder - actual path integrals are infinite-dimensional
    # Monte Carlo approximation over sampled configurations
    
    n_samples = len(P_configs)
    weights = np.zeros(n_samples)
    
    for i in range(n_samples):
        # Compute action for this configuration
        S = action_S(P_configs[i], B_configs[i], T_configs[i], 
                     W_configs[i], C_configs[i])
        weights[i] = np.exp(1j * S)
    
    # Partition function
    Z = np.sum(weights) / n_samples
    
    return Z


# Function 116: Neurodynamics Master Equation
def neurodynamics_master_equation(psi, D, V, K, dt=0.001, n_steps=1000):
    """
    ∂Ψ/∂t = (D∇² - V/ℏ + ∫ K|Ψ|²)Ψ
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    n_space = len(psi)
    psi_history = [psi.copy()]
    hbar = 1.0  # natural units
    
    for step in range(n_steps):
        # Kinetic term (diffusion)
        laplacian = np.zeros_like(psi)
        laplacian[1:-1] = (psi[2:] - 2*psi[1:-1] + psi[:-2])
        
        # Potential term
        potential_term = -V * psi / hbar
        
        # Interaction term (non-local convolution)
        interaction = np.zeros_like(psi, dtype=complex)
        for i in range(n_space):
            kernel_sum = 0
            for j in range(n_space):
                kernel_sum += K[i, j] * np.abs(psi[j])**2
            interaction[i] = kernel_sum * psi[i]
        
        # Update
        dpsi_dt = D * laplacian + potential_term + interaction
        psi += dt * dpsi_dt
        
        # Normalize
        psi = psi / np.sqrt(np.sum(np.abs(psi)**2))
        
        psi_history.append(psi.copy())
    
    return np.array(psi_history)


# Function 117: Criticality Scaling Law
def criticality_scaling_law(observable, rho_values, rho_c=1.0):
    """
    ⟨O⟩ ∼ |ρ - ρ_c|^(-β) as ρ → ρ_c
    """
    import numpy as np
    from scipy.optimize import curve_fit
    
    def scaling_law(rho, beta, C):
        return C * np.abs(rho - rho_c) ** (-beta)
    
    # Fit only near criticality
    near_critical = np.abs(rho_values - rho_c) < 0.1
    if np.sum(near_critical) < 3:
        return None
    
    rho_near = rho_values[near_critical]
    obs_near = observable[near_critical]
    
    try:
        popt, _ = curve_fit(scaling_law, rho_near, obs_near, p0=[0.5, 1.0])
        return {'beta': popt[0], 'C': popt[1]}
    except:
        return None


# Function 118: Federated Coherence Metric
def federated_coherence_metric(mutual_information, entropies, B_values, T_values, T_range=2.0):
    """
    CI_federated = (2/(N(N-1))) Σ (I(i;j)/(H(i)+H(j))) · e^(-|B_i-B_j|) · (1 - |T_i-T_j|/T_range)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    N = len(mutual_information)
    total = 0
    count = 0
    
    for i in range(N):
        for j in range(i+1, N):
            mi_term = mutual_information[i, j] / (entropies[i] + entropies[j] + 1e-10)
            B_term = np.exp(-np.abs(B_values[i] - B_values[j]))
            T_term = 1 - np.abs(T_values[i] - T_values[j]) / T_range
            T_term = max(0, T_term)
            
            total += mi_term * B_term * T_term
            count += 1
    
    if count > 0:
        CI_fed = (2 / (N * (N-1))) * total
    else:
        CI_fed = 0
    
    return CI_fed


# Function 119: Psychiatric State Space Metric
def psychiatric_state_space_metric(dP, dB, dT, g_PP=1.0, g_BB=1.0, g_TT=1.0,
                                   g_PB=0.1, g_PT=0.1, g_BT=0.1):
    """
    ds² = g_PP dP² + g_BB dB² + g_TT dT² + 2g_PB dPdB + 2g_PT dP dT + 2g_BT dB dT
    """
    ds2 = (g_PP * dP**2 + g_BB * dB**2 + g_TT * dT**2 +
           2 * g_PB * dP * dB + 2 * g_PT * dP * dT + 2 * g_BT * dB * dT)
    
    return ds2


# Function 120: Thermodynamic Cost of Consciousness
def thermodynamic_cost_consciousness(Q_heat, T, S_info):
    """
    S_brain = Q/T + S_info
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    S_brain = Q_heat / T + S_info
    
    return S_brain


# Function 121: Holographic Uncertainty Principle
def holographic_uncertainty_principle(dP, dB, dT, hbar_eff=1.0, alpha=0.1):
    """
    ΔP · ΔB ≥ (ħ_eff/2)(1 + α(ΔT)²)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    uncertainty_product = dP * dB
    lower_bound = (hbar_eff / 2) * (1 + alpha * dT**2)
    
    return uncertainty_product >= lower_bound, uncertainty_product, lower_bound


# Function 122: Unified Prediction Error Equation
def unified_prediction_error(hierarchical_errors, social_errors, correlation_errors,
                            beta_l, gamma_s, kappa):
    """
    δ_total = Σ β_l δ_l + Σ γ_s δ_s + ∫ κ(x) δ_corr(x) d⁴x
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Hierarchical terms
    hierarchical_total = np.sum([b * e for b, e in zip(beta_l, hierarchical_errors)])
    
    # Social terms
    social_total = np.sum([g * e for g, e in zip(gamma_s, social_errors)])
    
    # Correlation field term (integral approximated as sum)
    correlation_total = np.sum(kappa * correlation_errors)
    
    delta_total = hierarchical_total + social_total + correlation_total
    
    return delta_total


# Function 123: Coherence Wave Equation
def coherence_wave_equation(CI_field, source_term, social_current, m_CI=1.0, dt=0.01, n_steps=100):
    """
    □CI + m_CI² CI = J_source
    J_source = ρ_experience + ∇·J_social
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    n_space = len(CI_field)
    CI_history = [CI_field.copy()]
    
    for step in range(n_steps):
        # D'Alembertian (wave operator) in 1+1D simplified
        # ∂²/∂t² - ∂²/∂x² + m²
        laplacian = np.zeros_like(CI_field)
        laplacian[1:-1] = (CI_field[2:] - 2*CI_field[1:-1] + CI_field[:-2])
        
        # Time derivative (simplified - assuming small steps)
        if len(CI_history) > 1:
            d2dt2 = CI_field - 2*CI_history[-2] + CI_history[-3] if len(CI_history) > 2 else 0
        else:
            d2dt2 = 0
        
        box_CI = d2dt2 - laplacian + m_CI**2 * CI_field
        
        # Source term
        div_J_social = np.gradient(social_current)
        J_source = source_term + div_J_social
        
        # Update
        CI_new = CI_field + dt * (box_CI + J_source)
        CI_history.append(CI_new)
        CI_field = CI_new
    
    return np.array(CI_history)


# Function 124: Boundary Tunneling Probability
def boundary_tunneling_probability(V_x, E, mass, x1, x2, B):
    """
    P_tunnel ≈ e^(-2∫√(2m(V(x)-E))dx/ħ) · e^(-B)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # WKB tunneling amplitude (simplified)
    x = np.linspace(x1, x2, 100)
    V_x_vals = np.interp(x, np.arange(len(V_x)), V_x)
    
    integrand = np.sqrt(2 * mass * np.maximum(V_x_vals - E, 0))
    integral = np.trapz(integrand, x)
    
    hbar = 1.0
    tunneling = np.exp(-2 * integral / hbar)
    
    # Boundary modulation
    P_tunnel = tunneling * np.exp(-B)
    
    return P_tunnel


# Function 125: Temporal Horizon Operator
def temporal_horizon_operator(wavefunction, t_values, E_values, hbar_eff=1.0):
    """
    T̂ = ∫ t |t⟩⟨t| dt + iħ_eff ∂/∂E
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Time representation
    n_t = len(t_values)
    T_rep = np.diag(t_values)
    
    # Energy representation derivative (simplified finite diff)
    n_E = len(E_values)
    d_dE = np.zeros((n_E, n_E))
    for i in range(1, n_E-1):
        d_dE[i, i-1] = -1
        d_dE[i, i+1] = 1
    d_dE = d_dE / (2 * (E_values[1] - E_values[0]))
    
    # Combine (simplified - would need proper transformation between representations)
    T_operator = T_rep + 1j * hbar_eff * d_dE
    
    return T_operator


# Function 126: Social Field Equations
def social_field_equations(agent_density, phi_social, c_s=1.0, dt=0.01, n_steps=100):
    """
    ∇²φ - (1/c_s²) ∂²φ/∂t² = ρ_agents
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    n_space = len(phi_social)
    phi_history = [phi_social.copy()]
    
    for step in range(n_steps):
        # Spatial Laplacian
        laplacian = np.zeros_like(phi_social)
        laplacian[1:-1] = (phi_social[2:] - 2*phi_social[1:-1] + phi_social[:-2])
        
        # Time derivative (simplified)
        if len(phi_history) > 1:
            d2dt2 = phi_social - 2*phi_history[-2] + phi_history[-3] if len(phi_history) > 2 else 0
        else:
            d2dt2 = 0
        
        # Wave equation
        dphi_dt2 = c_s**2 * (laplacian - agent_density)
        
        # Update (using central difference for second order)
        if len(phi_history) > 1:
            phi_new = 2*phi_social - phi_history[-2] + dt**2 * dphi_dt2
        else:
            phi_new = phi_social + dt * np.zeros_like(phi_social)  # placeholder
        
        phi_history.append(phi_new)
        phi_social = phi_new
    
    return np.array(phi_history)
```

### Group 8 — Advanced Unified Formalizations (Functions 127-144)

```python
# Function 127: Neuroplasticity RG Flow
def neuroplasticity_renormalization_group(lambda_values, P, B, T, Lambda_scale, n_steps=10):
    """
    dλ/d ln Λ = β_λ(λ, P, B, T)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Beta function (simplified - would be derived from theory)
    def beta_lambda(lambda_val, P, B, T):
        return -lambda_val + 0.1 * P * lambda_val**2 - 0.05 * B * lambda_val + 0.01 * T
    
    lambda_history = [lambda_values.copy()]
    log_Lambda = np.log(Lambda_scale)
    d_log_Lambda = log_Lambda / n_steps
    
    for step in range(n_steps):
        new_lambda = []
        for i, lam in enumerate(lambda_values):
            # RG flow
            beta = beta_lambda(lam, P[i], B[i], T[i])
            lam_new = lam + beta * d_log_Lambda
            new_lambda.append(max(0, lam_new))  # ensure positivity
        
        lambda_values = np.array(new_lambda)
        lambda_history.append(lambda_values.copy())
    
    return np.array(lambda_history)


# Function 128: Unified Diagnostic Functional
def unified_diagnostic_functional(P_field, B_field, T_field, sigma_field, rho_field, r_field, d_s_field):
    """
    𝒟[Ψ] = ∫(αP² + βB² + γT² + δσ² + ε(ρ-1)² + ζ(r/d_s - 0.93)²) d³x
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    alpha, beta, gamma, delta, epsilon, zeta = 1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 1.0, 10.0, 10.0
    
    # Integrate over space
    integrand = (alpha * P_field**2 + beta * B_field**2 + gamma * T_field**2 +
                 delta * sigma_field**2 + epsilon * (rho_field - 1.0)**2 +
                 zeta * (r_field/d_s_field - 0.93)**2)
    
    diagnostic = np.trapz(integrand)
    
    return diagnostic


# Function 129: Healing Operator
def healing_operator(rho_state, H0, V_ops, lambda_vals, t_span, dt=0.01):
    """
    Ĥ_therapy = Ĥ₀ + Σ λ_i(t) V̂_i(t)
    Time-dependent perturbation theory
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    n_steps = int((t_span[1] - t_span[0]) / dt)
    n = rho_state.shape[0]
    rho_history = [rho_state.copy()]
    
    for step in range(n_steps):
        t = t_span[0] + step * dt
        
        # Construct time-dependent Hamiltonian
        H_t = H0.copy()
        for V, lambda_func in zip(V_ops, lambda_vals):
            H_t += lambda_func(t) * V
        
        # Unitary evolution (simplified)
        U = np.eye(n) - 1j * H_t * dt
        rho_new = U @ rho_state @ U.conj().T
        
        # Normalize
        rho_new = rho_new / np.trace(rho_new)
        
        rho_history.append(rho_new)
        rho_state = rho_new
    
    return np.array(rho_history)


# Function 130: Recursive Self-Consistency Condition
def recursive_self_consistency(psi_self, psi_world, psi_others, F_map, tolerance=1e-6, max_iter=100):
    """
    Ψ_self = F[Ψ_self, Ψ_world, Ψ_others]
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    psi_self_current = psi_self.copy()
    
    for iteration in range(max_iter):
        # Apply mapping
        psi_self_new = F_map(psi_self_current, psi_world, psi_others)
        
        # Check convergence
        diff = np.linalg.norm(psi_self_new - psi_self_current)
        if diff < tolerance:
            return psi_self_new, iteration, True
        
        psi_self_current = psi_self_new
    
    return psi_self_current, max_iter, False


# Function 131: Information-Geodesic Equation
def information_geodesic_equation(initial_point, fisher_metric, n_steps=100):
    """
    d²x^μ/dτ² + Γ^μ_νλ dx^ν/dτ dx^λ/dτ = 0
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # This is a placeholder - geodesic equation on information manifold
    # Would require computing Christoffel symbols from Fisher metric
    
    trajectory = [initial_point]
    velocity = np.random.randn(len(initial_point)) * 0.1
    
    for step in range(n_steps):
        # Compute Christoffel symbols (simplified - would be derived from metric)
        # Placeholder: move along gradient of Fisher information
        current = trajectory[-1]
        
        # Simplified geodesic: move in direction of decreasing Fisher info
        grad = np.gradient(fisher_metric(current))
        acceleration = -grad
        
        velocity += acceleration * 0.01
        new_point = current + velocity * 0.01
        
        trajectory.append(new_point)
    
    return np.array(trajectory)


# Function 132: Holographic Bound on Learning
def holographic_learning_bound(synaptic_area, brain_temperature, l_P=1.0, k_B=1.0):
    """
    I_learned ≤ (A_synaptic / 4l_P²) · 1/(k_B T_brain)
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    bound = (synaptic_area / (4 * l_P**2)) * 1 / (k_B * brain_temperature)
    
    return bound


# Function 133: Consciousness-Field Coupling
def consciousness_field_coupling(psi_mind, phi_field, coupling_strength=1.0):
    """
    ℒ_int = g ψ†_mind Φ_field ψ_mind
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Interaction Lagrangian density
    L_int = coupling_strength * np.conj(psi_mind) * phi_field * psi_mind
    
    return L_int


# Function 134: Unified Observer Equation
def unified_observer_equation(O_self, O_others, O_cosmic):
    """
    O_total = O_self + Σ O_others + O_cosmic
    """
    O_total = O_self + np.sum(O_others) + O_cosmic
    
    return O_total


# Function 135: Final Unified Equation of Everything (Mental)
def final_unified_equation(H_QM, H_GR, H_CC, H_UTD, H_UHG, H_UHIF, H_social, psi_universe, hbar=1.0):
    """
    Ĥ_total|Ψ⟩ = iħ ∂/∂t |Ψ⟩
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    H_total = (H_QM + H_GR + H_CC + H_UTD + H_UHG + H_UHIF + H_social)
    
    # Time evolution
    def time_evolve(psi, t, dt):
        # Simplified evolution operator
        U = np.eye(len(psi)) - 1j * H_total * dt / hbar
        psi_new = U @ psi
        return psi_new / np.linalg.norm(psi_new)
    
    return H_total, time_evolve


# Function 136: Relational Ontology Axiom
def relational_ontology_axiom(correlation_matrix, epsilon=0.01):
    """
    ∃x ⇔ ∃y: Corr(x,y) > ε
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    n = correlation_matrix.shape[0]
    exists = np.zeros(n, dtype=bool)
    
    for i in range(n):
        # Check if correlated with any other entity
        correlated = np.any(np.abs(correlation_matrix[i, :]) > epsilon)
        exists[i] = correlated
    
    return exists


# Function 137: Coherence Conservation Axiom
def coherence_conservation_axiom(CI_current, source_terms, sink_terms):
    """
    ∇_μ J_CI^μ = Σ_source - Σ_sink
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Divergence of coherence current
    divergence = np.gradient(CI_current)
    
    # Conservation equation
    balance = divergence - (source_terms - sink_terms)
    
    return balance


# Function 138: Criticality Principle
def criticality_principle(rho_values, n_systems):
    """
    lim_{N→∞} P(consciousness) = 1 ⇔ ρ = 1 ± ε
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Probability of consciousness given spectral radius
    def P_consciousness(rho, N, epsilon=0.05):
        if np.abs(rho - 1.0) < epsilon:
            return 1 - np.exp(-N / 1000)  # approaches 1 as N increases
        else:
            return np.exp(-N * np.abs(rho - 1.0))  # approaches 0 as N increases
    
    probs = [P_consciousness(rho, n_systems) for rho in rho_values]
    
    return probs


# Function 139: Holographic Encoding Theorem
def holographic_encoding_theorem(psi_mind, boundary_operator):
    """
    ∀Ψ_mind, ∃∂M: Ψ_mind = Ψ_boundary
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Map bulk state to boundary
    psi_boundary = boundary_operator @ psi_mind
    
    # Check if mapping is invertible (simplified)
    try:
        psi_reconstructed = np.linalg.pinv(boundary_operator) @ psi_boundary
        fidelity = np.abs(np.vdot(psi_mind, psi_reconstructed))**2
        return fidelity > 0.99  # High fidelity means holographic encoding holds
    except:
        return False


# Function 140: Federated Coherence Theorem
def federated_coherence_theorem(CI_values, network_adjacency, threshold=0.01):
    """
    Σ CI_i = constant ⇔ network closed
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Check if network is closed (no connections to outside)
    external_connections = np.sum(network_adjacency, axis=1) - np.diag(network_adjacency)
    is_closed = np.all(external_connections < threshold)
    
    # Total coherence
    total_CI = np.sum(CI_values)
    
    return total_CI, is_closed


# Function 141: Temporal Arrow of Consciousness
def temporal_arrow_consciousness(S_mind_history):
    """
    dS_mind/dt ≥ 0 ⇒ psychological time's arrow
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Entropy change
    dS_dt = np.gradient(S_mind_history)
    
    # Arrow direction
    arrow_forward = np.all(dS_dt >= -0.01 * np.std(dS_dt))  # allow small fluctuations
    
    return arrow_forward, dS_dt


# Function 142: Quantum-Classical Bridge
def quantum_classical_bridge(H_quantum, hbar=1.0):
    """
    lim_{ħ→0} Ĥ_quantum = H_classical + H_mental
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Classical limit by taking hbar small
    hbar_small = 0.01
    H_classical_approx = H_quantum * (hbar_small / hbar)
    
    # Mental term emerges from quantum effects
    H_mental = H_quantum - H_classical_approx
    
    return H_classical_approx, H_mental


# Function 143: Unification Identity
def unification_identity(P, B, T, sigma, rho, r, lambda_val, T_c, tau_u):
    """
    P · B · T · σ · ρ · r · λ · T_c · τ_u = constant
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    product = P * B * T * sigma * rho * r * lambda_val * T_c * tau_u
    
    # Constant should be invariant across scales
    return product


# Function 144: Omega Point Equation
def omega_point_equation(F_total_history):
    """
    lim_{t→∞} F_total(t) = F_min
    """
    import numpy as np
    
    # Extrapolate to infinite time
    t = np.arange(len(F_total_history))
    
    # Fit exponential decay to minimum
    from scipy.optimize import curve_fit
    
    def decay_func(t, F_min, F0, tau):
        return F_min + (F0 - F_min) * np.exp(-t / tau)
    
    try:
        popt, _ = curve_fit(decay_func, t, F_total_history, 
                           p0=[np.min(F_total_history), F_total_history[0], 100])
        F_min, F0, tau = popt
        
        # Limit as t→∞
        F_inf = F_min
        
        return F_inf, F0, tau
    except:
        return np.min(F_total_history), F_total_history[0], None
```

# SECTION 14.0: MASTER SYNTHESIS
## Unified Field Equation of Hyper-Correlational Processing

### The Grounded Mind-State Prediction Function

$$\boxed{ \Psi_{\text{mind}}(t) = \mathcal{F}\left( \mathcal{P}(t), \mathcal{B}(t), \mathcal{T}(t), \int_0^t \mathbf{W}(\tau) d\tau, \mathbf{S}(t) \right) + \epsilon(t) }$$

Where:

| Variable | Definition | Measurement | Units |
|----------|------------|-------------|-------|
| \(\mathcal{P}(t)\) | Precision axis | EEG MMN SNR | \(\mu V \cdot ms^{-1}\) |
| \(\mathcal{B}(t)\) | Boundary axis | fMRI DMN FC ratio | dimensionless |
| \(\mathcal{T}(t)\) | Temporal axis | Delay-discounting log-k z-score | dimensionless |
| \(\mathbf{W}(\tau)\) | Functional connectivity matrix | 30s sliding-window EEG | dimensionless correlations |
| \(\mathbf{S}(t)\) | Sensory input vector | Stimulus features | normalized |
| \(\mathcal{F}\) | Nonlinear function | XGBoost, neural ODE, Gaussian Process | - |
| \(\epsilon(t)\) | Prediction error | \(\epsilon \sim \mathcal{N}(0, \sigma_\epsilon^2)\) | same as target |

### Model Fitting Protocol

**Training Data:** N = 80 subjects × 30-min multimodal recording (EEG + fMRI + behavioral)

**Target Variables:**
- Self-reported state (valence, arousal, social connection on 7-point Likert scales)
- Behavioral accuracy on social inference task

**Validation:** 10-fold stratified cross-validation; report mean R² ± SD across folds

**Baseline Comparison:** Predict target from P alone, B alone, T alone; test if full model significantly improves (ΔR² > 0.10, F-test p < 0.01)

**Overfitting Check:** Compare training R² vs. test R²; if difference > 0.15, regularize or reduce features
